관리자(웹)

form은 제외함

1. 관리자 로그인

Request Example
POST /loginAdmin HTTP/1.1
Host: localhost:8080
Content-Type: application/x-www-form-urlencoded

email=admin%40naver.com&password=1234
Response Example
HTTP/1.1 302 Found
Content-Language: en
Location: /
